+Jamison Brereton

23 (214)
Br╠еhaspati
Gr╠еtsamada
19 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 15, 19
The relation between the god Br╠еhaspati and Indra is fluid within the R╠еgveda. As Schmidt (1968) has demonstrated, br╠е╠Бhasp├бti and br├бhmanas p├бti тАЬlord of the sacred formulationтАЭ are usually names of Indra in the context of the Vala myth. At times, however, Br╠еhaspati emerges as an independent deity, though closely linked to Indra. Here the poet once describes Br╠еhaspati as the тАЬyokemateтАЭ of Indra (vs. 18), but beyond this statement, there is otherwise little to distinguish Indra and Br╠еhaspati.
Framing the hymnтАЩs description of Br╠еhaspati are overt references to the Vala myth, in which Indra as Br╠еhaspati leads the Aс╣Еgirases and, by the power of their song, opens the cave that releases the cattle and dawns (vss. 2, 3, 18). The interme diate verses expand the theme of the power of the verbal formulation, of which Br╠еhaspati is the master. It is by means of knowledge of the truth that Br╠еhaspati and the poet, who possesses mastery of the truth through Br╠еhaspati, are able to overcome their enemies. They defeat scorners (vs. 8), slighters (vs. 13), chatterers (vs. 14), and speakers of ill (vs. 10). They overcome those who hate the real for mulations of the truth (vs. 4), who lay snares (vs. 6), and who are deceitful (vss. 5, 16, 17). Perhaps because of his powerful speech, Br╠еhaspatiтАЩs mouth even тАЬsnaps atтАЭ the poetтАЩs enemies (vs. 9). At least in some instances, the rivals of the poet are rival sacrificers. At best, however, these know the words to recite, but not the truth that produces the songs or that lies behind them (vs. 16). Through the truth and the truth formulations, the poet and his people are freed from distress (vs. 4), hostility (vss. 5, 9), and injury (vss. 7, 8, 12) and instead prosper (vss. 10, 15).

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬWe invoke the Brahmaс╣Зaspati, chief leaderof the (heavenly) bands; a sage of sage; aboundingbeyondmeasure in (every kind of) food;best lord of prayer; hearing our invocations, come with your protections, and sit down in the chamber of sacrifice.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Brahmaс╣Зaspati = brahmaс╣Зo annasya parivс╣Ыс╕Нhasya karmaс╣Зo v─Б p─Бlayit─Б, the protector or cherisher of food,or of any great or solemn acts of devotion; he has other attributes in the text, as, gaс╣З─Бn─Бm gaс╣Зapatiс╕е, chief of the gaс╣Зas (inferior deities); jyeс╣гс╣нhar─Бjam brahmaс╣З─Бm, the best lord of mantras, or prayers: pra┼Ыasyam sv─Бminam mantr─Бс╣З─Бm

We call upon you, the troop-lord of troops, the most famous poet of poets,
the preeminent king of sacred formulations, o lord of the sacred
formulation. Hearing us, sit down upon your seat together with your help.

WE call thee, Lord and Leader of the heavenly hosts, the wise among the wise, the famousest of all,
The King supreme of prayers, O Brahmanaspati: hear us with help; sit down in place of sacrifice.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬBс╣Ыhaspati, destroyer of the asuras, through you the intelligent gods have obtained the sacrificialportion; in like manner as the adorable sun genitive rates the (solar) rays by his radiance, so are you the genitive rator of all prayers.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Bс╣Ыhaspati = Brahmaс╣Зaspati; perhaps Bс╣Ыhaspati is of a more martial character; his protection is souhght for against enemies and evil spirits; perhaps, bс╣Ыhat─Бm ved─Бn─Бm p─Бlakaс╕е: bс╣Ыhat = mantra, bс╣Ыhato mantrasya, sv─Бmin

+Jamison Brereton

Even the prescient gods attained their sacrificial portion from you, lordly Br╠еhaspati.
As the great sun is (the begetter) of ruddy dawn through its light, you are the very begetter of all formulations.

+Griffith

Brhaspati, God immortal! verily the Gods have gained from thee, the wise, a share in holy rites.
As with great light the Sun brings forth the rays of morn, so thou alone art Father of all sacred prayer.

+Geldner

Die weisen G├╢tter selbst haben von dir, du asurischer Brihaspati, ihren Anteil am Opfer empfangen. Wie die gro├Яe Sonne durch ihr Licht die Morgenr├╢te, so erzeugest du alle Segensworte.

+Grassmann

Die weisen G├╢tter, himmlischer Gebetes Herr; erlangten g├╢ttliche Verehrung erst durch dich; Wie gross an Glanz die Sonne Morgenr├╢then zeugt, so bist du Zeuger aller frommen Bitten auch.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬHaving repelled revilers and (dispersed) the darkness you stand Bс╣Ыhaspati, on the radiant chariot of sacrifice, (which is) formidable (to foes), the humiliator of enemies, the destroyer of evil spirits, the cleaver of the clouds, the attainer of heaven.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Having pressed away evasive chatter and darkness, you mount truthтАЩs light-bearing chariot,
which terrifies, which vanquishes enemies, o Br╠еhaspati, and which
smashes demons, splits cowpens, and finds the sun.

+Griffith

When thou hast chased away revilers and the gloom, thou mountest the refulgent car of sacrifice;
The awful car, Brhaspati, that quells the foe, slays demons, cleaves the stall of kine, and finds the light.

+Geldner

Indem du die Ausreden und die Finsternis des Herzens zerstreust, besteigest du den lichten Wagen des Gesetzes, o Brihaspati, den furchtbaren, der die Feinde ├╝berlistet, die Unholde t├╢tet, die Kuhh├╢hle aufsprengt, das Himmelslicht findet.

+Grassmann

Die Dunkel jagend und die grausig summenden, besteigst den hellen Wagen du des Opferwerks, Den hehren, welcher Feinde tilgt, Gebetes Herr, Gespenster t├╢dtet, Heerden schenkt und Glanz verschafft.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬYou lead men, Bс╣Ыhaspati, by virtuous instrumental uctions; you preserve them (from calamity); sin will never overtake him who presents (offerings) to you; you are the afflicter of him who hates (holy) prayers; you are the punisher of wrath; such is your great mightiness.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Him who hates holy prayers: brahmadviс╣гaс╕е = those who hate either the br─Бhmaс╣Зas,or the mantras or prayers

+Jamison Brereton

You guide with good guidance, and you rescue the man who will do (ritual) service for you. Distress will not reach him.
Confounding his fury, you are the scorcher of him who hates the sacred formulation. Br╠еhaspati, great is that greatness of yours.

+Griffith

Thou leadest with good guidance and preservest men; distress o’ertakes not him who offers gifts to thee.
Him who hates prayer thou punishest, Brhaspati, quelling his wrath: herein is thy great mightiness.

+Geldner

Mit guten Weisungen leitest du, sch├╝tzest du den Mann, der dir zu spenden pflegt; ihn soll keine Not treffen. Du schaffst brennende Pein, du vereitelst den b├╢sen Eifer des Feindes des Priesterworts: Das ist deine hehre Gr├╢├Яe, o Brihaspati.

+Grassmann

Durch sch├╢ne Leitung leitest, rettest du den Mann; der dich verehret, nicht erreicht Bedr├дngniss den; Die Andachthasser brennend, hemmst du ihre Wuth; das ist, Gebets Herr, deine grosse Allgewalt.

+Elizarenkova

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬThe man whom you, Brahmaс╣Зaspati, a kind protector, defend, neither sorrow nor sin, nor adversaries nor dissemblers ever harm, for you drive away from him all injurious (things).тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Neither distress nor difficulty from anywhere overcomes him, nor hostilities nor the duplicitous ones.
You press away all that harms from him whom you protect as his good herdsman, o lord of the sacred formulation.

+Griffith

No sorrow, no distress from any side, no foes, no creatures double-tongued have overcome the man,-
Thou drivest all seductive fiends away from him whom, careful guard, thou keepest Brahmanaspati.

+Geldner

English translation:

тАЬYou, Bс╣Ыhaspati, are our protector and the guide of (our) path; (you are) the discerner (of all things); we worship with praises for your adoration; may his own precipitate malice involve him (in destruction) who practises deceit against us.тАЭ

You are our herdsman, creating paths and seeing afar. We are awake to your command with our thoughts.
Br╠еhaspati, let grasping disaster, rightfully his, grind to pieces him who sets a snare for us.

+Griffith

Thou art our keeper, wise, preparer of our paths: we, for thy service, sing to thee with hymns of praise.
Brhaspati, whoever lays a snare for us, him may his evil fate, precipitate, destroy.

Du bist ein weitblickender Hirte und Wegebereiter. Zu deinem Dienste sind wir mit Liedern wach. Brihaspati, wer uns eine Falle stellt, den soll sein eigenes Unheil wutentbrannt zermalmen.

+Grassmann

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬTurn aside from (the true) path, Bс╣Ыhaspati, the arrogant and savage man who advances to injure us, although unoffending and keep us in the right way for (the completion of) this offering to the gods.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Or if a hostile mortal, a lone wolf, is about to injure us who are without offense,
Br╠еhaspati, turn him away from our path. Make an easy way for this our pursuit of the gods.

+Griffith

Him, too, who threatens us without offence of ours, the evilminded, arrogant, rapacious man,-
Him turn thou from our path away, Brhaspati: give us fair access to this banquet of the Gods.

+Grassmann

Und den auch, der unschuld’ge uns besch├дdiget, den schlechtgesinnten Sterblichen, den gier’gen Wolf, Den, o Gebets Herr, wende ab von unserm Pfad, und schaffe guten Zugang uns zum G├╢ttermahl.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬBс╣Ыhaspati, defender (from calamity), we invoke you, the protector of our person ns, the speaker of encouraging words and well disposed towards us; do you destroy the revilers of the gods; let not the malevolent attain supreme felicity.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

We call upon you as the rescuer of our bodies, as our defender who inclines toward us, o deliverer.
Br╠еhaspati, lay low those who scorn the gods. Let evil-doers not gain higher favor.434 II.23

+Griffith

Thee as protector of our bodies we invoke, thee, saviour, as the comforter who loveth us.
Strike, O Brhaspati, the Gods’ revilers down, and let not the unrighteous come to highest bliss.

+Geldner

Wir rufen dich als den Sch├╝tzer der Leiber an, als den uns g├╝nstigen F├╝rsprecher, du Befreier. O Brihaspati, schmettere die G├╢tterschm├дher nieder. Nicht sollen die B├╢swilligen h├╢here Gunst als wir erlangen.

+Grassmann

Dich, den Besch├╝tzer unsrer Leiber rufen wir, Erretter du, der holdgesinnt f├╝r uns du sprichst; Die G├╢tterhasser st├╝rz herab Gebetes Herr; nicht B├╢sgesinnte lass erlangen h├╢h’re Huld.

+Elizarenkova

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬThrough you, Bс╣Ыhaspati, (who are) the fulfiller of our desires; pure, and associated (with us), we possess excellent food; let not the wicked man who wishes to deceive us be our master; but let us, excelling in (pious) praises, attain (prosperity).тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

Through you, o Br╠еhaspati, we would receive the utmost vigorтАФyou, our providing, winning yokemate.
Let not the speaker of ill, trying to deceive, be master of us. As speakers of good, we would advance through our thoughts.

+Griffith

With thee as our own rich and liberal ally may we, Brhaspati, gain highest power of life.
Let not the guileful wicked man be lord of us:-still may we prosper, singing goodly hymns of praise.

+Geldner

Durch dich den reichlich spendenden und lohnenden Verb├╝ndeten m├╢chten wir h├╢chste Lebenskraft erlangen, o Brihaspati. Nicht soll der ├Ьbelredende, Schadens├╝chtige ├╝ber uns Macht haben. Wir m├╢chten als Belobte durch unsere Gedichte vorw├дrtskommen.

+Grassmann

Durch dich erlangen wir die h├╢chste Lebenskraft; Brihaspati, durch dich, der viel gewinnt und schenkt; Nicht herrsch ein b├╢ser, hinterlistger ├╝ber uns; wir gutgesinnten seien siegreich durch Gebet.

+Elizarenkova

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬYou, Brahmaс╣Зaspati, who have no requiter (of your bounty), who are the showerer (of benefits), the repairer to combat, the consumer of foes, the victor in battles, you are true, the discharger of debts, the humiliator of the fierce and of the exulting.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

You are a bull unable to be pushed aside, going toward a challenge, scorcher of his rival and overwhelming in battles,
the real redeemer of debts, o lord of the sacred formulation, and the tamer even of the powerful one, excited to tough resistance.

+Griffith

Strong, never yielding, hastening to the battle-cry, consumer of the foe, victorious in the strife,
Thou art sin’s true avenger, Brahmanaspati, who tamest e’en the fierce, the wildly passionate.

+Geldner

Ein unnachgiebiger Bulle, gern in den Streit ziehend, ein Ausbrenner des Feindes, in den Schlachten siegreich, bist du der wahrhafte Vergelter, o Brahmanaspati, der Bezwinger selbst des Gewaltigen, der sich seiner H├дrte freut.

+Grassmann

Ein Held bist du, der nimmer weichend eilt zum Kampf, den Feind verbrennend, in den Schlachten sieggewohnt, Schuldr├дcher bist du, treugesinnt, Gebetes Herr, auch des gewalt’gen, kraftbewussten B├дndiger.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬConsume with your brightest (weapon) the r─Бkс╣гasas, who have held your witnessed prowess in disdain; manifest, Bс╣Ыhaspati, your glorified (vigour), such as it was (of old), and destroy those who speak against you.тАЭ

+Jamison Brereton

With your sharpest scorching, scorch the demons who have put you of manifest heroism to scorn.
Reveal that of yours which will be worthy of a hymn. Shake evasive chatter to pieces, Br╠еhaspati.

+Griffith

Burn up the demons with thy fiercest flaming brand, those who have scorned thee in thy manifested might.
Show forth that power that shall deserve the hymn of praise: destroy the evil speakers, O Brhaspati.

+Geldner

+Grassmann

Mit sch├дrfster Glut verbrenne der Gespenster Schar, die der Verachtung dich, den krafterprobten, weihn; Was r├╝hmenswerthes dein ist, das mach offenbar, Brihaspati zerspreng’ die grausig summenden.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬBс╣Ыhaspati, born of truth, grant us that wonderful treasure, wherewith the pious man may worship exceedingly; that (wealth) which shines amongst men; which is endowed with lustre, (is) the means of (performing holy) rites, and invogirates (its possessor) with strength.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Draviс╣Зam citram = liс╣н, various or wonderful wealth; in the Br─Бhmaс╣Зas it is interpreted as brahma varcas or tejas, brahmanical virtue or energy (cf. Yajus. 26.3;

Draviс╣Зam = dhanam (Aitareya Br─Бhmaс╣Зa 4.11)

+Jamison Brereton

Br╠еhaspati! That which will be worth more than what belongs to the stranger, (that which) will radiate among the peoples with brilliance and purpose,
and that which will shine by means of your power, o you born through the truthтАФset that shimmering possession among us.

+Griffith

Brhaspati, that which the foe deserves not which shines among the folk effectual, splendid,
That, Son of Law I which is with might refulgent-that treasure wonderful bestow thou on us.

+Geldner

Brihaspati, gib uns den wunderbaren Schatz, der mehr wert sei als der des hohen Herrn, der unter den Menschen lichtvoll, weisheitsvoll erstrahlt, der m├дchtig leuchtet, du Wahrheitgeborener.

+Grassmann

Brihaspati, was recht dem Frommen werth gilt, was gl├дnzend strahlt und wirksam unter Menschen, Was kr├дftig leuchtet, heil’gen Werks entsprossner, das schenke du als gl├дnzenden Besitz uns.

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬDeliver us not to the thieves, the enemies delighting in violence, who seize ever upon the food (of others); those who cherish in their hearts the abandonment (of the gods); (they), Bс╣Ыhaspati, who do not know the extent of (your) power (against evil spirits).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Who do not know the extenf of your power: na paraс╕е s─Бmno viduс╕е = ye pum─Бmsaс╕е s─Бmnaс╕е s─Бmay─Бt tvattaс╕е paraс╕е parast─Бd anyadukс╣Ыс╣гс╣нam s─Бma yad rakс╣гoghnam na j─Бnanti, those men who do not know anything greater than the faculty of destroying r─Бkс╣гasas, derived from you made up of that faculty; s─Бma vai rakс╣гoha = s─Бma is the killer of r─Бkс╣гasas

+Jamison Brereton

(Give) us not to thieves, the cheats, lurking in the track of deceit, who have become greedy for our supplies
and (who) declare the crushing power of the gods (but set it) aside in their heart. Br╠еhaspati, they do not know (anything) beyond the s─Бman-chant (itself).

+Griffith

Give us not up to those who, foes in ambuscade, are greedy for the wealth of him who sits at ease,
Who cherish in their heart abandonment of Gods. Brhaspati, no further rest shall they obtain.

+Geldner

Gib uns nicht den R├дubern preis, die, sich an die Spuren der Falschheit h├дngend, als Betr├╝ger nach den Speisen gierig sind. Sie behaupten die Schw├дche der G├╢tter und leugnen die Schw├дche in ihrem eigenen Herzen. O Brihaspati, sie wissen nichts weiter als ihren Saman.

+Grassmann

Nicht gib uns hin den Dieben, die im Hinterhalt heimt├╝ckisch lauernd nach der Nahrung l├╝stern sind; Sich nicht im Herzen k├╝mmern um der G├╢tter Zorn, Brihaspati, die achten auch der Lieder nicht.

+Elizarenkova

рд╣реЗрдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордгрд╕реНрдкрддреЗ рддреНрд╡рд╖реНрдЯрд╛рдкреНрд░рдЬрд╛рдкрддрд┐рдГ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡реЗрднреНрдпреЛрднреБрд╡рдиреЗрднреНрдпрд╕реНрдкрд░рд┐рд╕рд░реНрд╡реЗрднреНрдпреЛрднреВрддрдЬрд╛рддреЗрднреНрдпрдГ рдЙрддреНрдХреГрд╖реНрдЯрдиреНрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреНрд╡рд╛рдВ рдЕрдЬрди рджреНрдзрд┐ рдЕрдЬреАрдЬрдирддреН рдЦрд▓реБ рддрддрд╕реНрддреНрд╡рдВрд╕рд╛рдореНрдирдГрд╕рд╛рдореНрдирдГ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкрд┐рд╕рд╛рдореНрдирдГрдХрд╡рд┐рдГ рдХреБрд╢рдмреНрджреЗ рдЕрдЪрдЗрд░рд┐рддрд┐рдЗрдорддреНрдпрдпрдГ рдЙрдЪреНрдЪрд╛рд░рдпрд┐ рддрд╛рдХрд╛рд░реНрддрд╛рд╕рд┐ рдпрджреНрд╡рд╛ рдХрд╡рд┐рдГрдХреНрд░рд╛рдиреНрддрджрд░реНрд╢реАрддреНрд╡рд╖реНрдЯрд╛рд╕рд╛рдореНрдирдГрд╕рд╛рдореНрдирдГ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╕реНрдпрд╛рдкрд┐рд╕рд╛рдореНрдирд╛рдГ рд╕рд╛рд░реЗрдг рддреНрд╡рд╛рдордЬреАрдЬрдирддреН рдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪ рд╕рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордгрд╕реНрдкрддрд┐рдГ рдорд╣реЛрдорд╣рддрдЛрддрд╕реНрдпрдпрдЬреНрдЮрдзрд░реНрддрд░рд┐ рдзрд╛рд░рдХреЗрдпрдЬрдорд╛рдиреЗрдЛрдгрдЪрд┐рддреН рд╕реНрддреЛрддреГрдХрд╛рдордореГрдгрдорд┐рд╡рдЪрд┐рдиреЛрддреАрддрд┐ рдЛрдгрдЪрд┐рддреН рдХрд┐рдЮреНрдЪ рдЛрдгрдпрд╛рдГ рдкрд╛рдкрд░реВрдкрд╕реНрдпрдЛрдгрд╕реНрдпрдпрд╛рд╡реНрдпрд┐рддрд╛рдкреГрдердХреНрдХрд░реНрддрд╛рдЪрджреНрд░реБрд╣рдГ рдХрд░реНрдордгреЛрджреНрд░реЛрдЧреНрдзреБрд░рд╕реБрд░рд╕реНрдпрд╣рдиреНрддрд╛рднрд╡реЗрддрд┐ рее рен рее

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬTvaс╣гс╣н─Б engendered you (chief) amongst all beings, (whence) you are the reciter of many a holy hymn: Brahmaс╣Зaspati acknowledges a debt to the performer of a sacred rite; he is the acquitter (of the debt), and the destoyer of the oppressor.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

When you are the reciter: s─Бmnaс╕е s─Бmnaс╕е kaviс╕е, the reicter or another of every s─Бma, sarvasya s─Бmnaс╕е ucc─Бrayit─Б kart─Бsi; or kavi refers to tvaс╣гс╣н─Б, further explained as the sage who created Brahmaс╣Зaspati by the efficacy of the s─Бma: s─Бmnaс╕е s─Бreс╣Зa tvam aj─лjanat; acknowledges a debt: с╣Ыс╣Зacit stotс╣Ыk─Бmam с╣Ыс╣Зam iva cinoti, he takes the intention of the praiser as if it was a debt, or obligation; acquitter of the debt: с╣Ыс╣Зaya is explained as the discharger or remover of the debt which is of the nature of sin: p─Бpar┼лpasya с╣Ыс╣Зasya pс╣Ыthak kart─Б

+Jamison Brereton

Since the sage Tvaс╣гс╣нar gave birth to you from all beings and from each s─Бman-chant,
so then (you), as the lord of the sacred formulation, are the collector of debts and redeemer of debts, and the smasher of deceit in your upholding of the great truth.

+Griffith

For Tvastar, he who knows each sacred song, brought thee to life, preeminent o’er all the things that be.
Guilt-scourger, guilt-avenger is Brhaspati, who slays the spoiler and upholds the mighty Law.

+Geldner

Denn aus allen Wesen erschuf dich der Seher Tvastri, aus einem jeden Saman. Brahmanaspati ist der Vergelter, der Schuldeinzieher, der Vernichter der Falschheit, der Erhalter der hohen Wahrheit.

+Grassmann

Denn aus den Wesen allen brachte dich hervor der weise Tvaschtar und aus allen Liedern dich; Brihaspati, der Schulden r├дcht und Schuld verfolgt, vertilgt die Hexen zu des grossen Rechtes Schutz.

+Elizarenkova

+Wilson
English translation:

тАЬBrahmaс╣Зaspati, who are the regulator of this (world), understand (the purport) of (our) hymn, and grant us posterity; for all is prosperous that the gods protect; (and therefore) may we blessed with excellent descendants, glorify you at this sacrifice.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Yajus. 34.58;

Vadema = may we declare or glorify you; or, let us speak, let what we ask be given to us;let it be enjoyed by us: d─лyat─Бm bhujyat─Бm ucc─Бrayema

+Jamison Brereton

Lord of the sacred formulation, become the guide of this hymn and give life to our lineage.
All that is fortunate which the gods aid. тАУ May we speak loftily at the ritual distribution, in possession of good heroes.

+Griffith

O Brahmanaspati, be thou controller of this our hymn and prosper thou our children.
All that the Gods regard with love is blessed. Loud may we speak, with heroes, in assembly.

+Geldner

O Brahmanaspati, sei du der Lenker dieses Liedes und erwecke Nachkommenschaft! Alles das ist l├╢blich, was die G├╢tter beg├╝nstigen. - Wir m├╢chten das gro├Яe Wort f├╝hren als Meister in weiser Rede.

+Grassmann

Gebetes Herr, sei dieses Liedes Lenker, und Kindeskinder m├╢gest du uns schaffen; voll Heil ist alles, was die G├╢tter segnen; lasst laut im Chore bei dem Fest uns singen.
